      31             : namespace boost{ namespace math{ namespace lanczos{
      32             : 
      33             : //
      34             : // Individual lanczos approximations start here.
      35             : //
      36             : // Optimal values for G for each N are taken from
      37             : // http://web.mala.bc.ca/pughg/phdThesis/phdThesis.pdf,
      38             : // as are the theoretical error bounds.
      39             : //
      40             : // Constants calculated using the method described by Godfrey
      41             : // http://my.fit.edu/~gabdo/gamma.txt and elaborated by Toth at
      42             : // http://www.rskey.org/gamma.htm using NTL::RR at 1000 bit precision.
      43             : //
      44             : //
      45             : // Non-member helper which allows us to have a different g() value for the
      46             : // near_1 and near_2 approximations.  This is a big help in reducing error
      47             : // rates for multiprecision types at large digit counts.
      48             : // Default version assumes all g() values are the same.
      49             : //
      50             : template <class L>
      51             : BOOST_MATH_GPU_ENABLED inline double lanczos_g_near_1_and_2(const L&)
      52             : {
      53             :    return L::g();
      54             : }
      55             :
